 aisa rahaa he scindia kaa raajnneetik safar2004: maharashtra vidhansabha ke liye chune gaye2009: maharashtra vidhansabha ke liye chune gaye2014: maharashtra vidhansabha ke liye chune gaoctober 2014-disambar 2014: maharashtra vidhansabha main vipaksh ke netaa2014: maharashtra rajya sarkaar main PWD ke cabinet mantri ke rup main niyukt2018: shivasena ke netaa ke rup main niyukt2019: cabinet mantri saarvajanik swasthya or parivaar kalyaan mantri (maharashtra sarkaar)31 oktober 2019: guuruuvaar ke din vidhansabha main shivasena kaa netaa chunaa gaya The National Register of Citizens of Assam (NRC) is very much discussed
 is par kaaphi raajnneeti or vaad-vivaad ho rahaa he
 It is being said that Assam is the first state to take initiative in the matter of NRC and now there is a demand to bring NRC in other states as well
 lekin aapako yah jaanakar achraj hoga ki desh ke sabhi rajyon main pehle hi enarasi taiyaar ho chukaa he
 Let's know what is the truth
 
 
 asal main desh ke bantwaare ke baad yah jaananaa jaruri tha ki desh main kitne log vaid yaa avaidh tareeke se rahe hai
 Therefore, in the year 1951 after independence, a National Register of Citizens was prepared across the country
 yah sabhi rajyon main taiyaar kiya gaya
 In this way, the NRC that is being prepared in Assam is not new, but only the NRC of 1951 is being updated
 saal 1951 main desh bhar main janaganana hui thi, jisamen har gaanv main sabhi makaanon kii kramvaar order ke mutabik jaankaree or usamen kitne log rahete hai, yah jaankaree hasil hui thi
 After this, the National Register of Citizens was prepared with the help of this census
 is register ko taiyaar karne ke baad ise centre sarkaar ke nirdesh par sabhi ilaakon ke dipti kamishnar or esadm ke daftaron main rakhaa gaya
 Later in the 1960s these registers were handed over to the Police Department
 kya he assam kaa enarasiasam kaa enarasi asal main saal 1951 main bane enarasi ko apadet karne kii hi kavayad he
 This includes all those whose names are included in the electoral rolls before 1971 or the NRC of 1951
 assam main kaise aage badha enarasi apadet karne kaa kafasal main sabhi rajyon main 1951 main jo enarasi taiyaar kii gai thi, vah janaganana par aadhaarit thi, isamen logon kaa samuchit veriphication nahin kiya gaya tha
 In this way, the upgrading of NRC in Assam has also been done for the first time in any state with such verification of citizenship
 1980 ke dashak main assam main avaidh logon ko baahar karne kaa ek bada andolan hua
 The All Assam Students Union gave a memorandum to the Prime Minister, seeking to update the NRC of 1951
 lekin iske baad 1985 main hue assam samjhaute main enarasi ke apadet karne kii baat shaamil nahin kii gai
 In 1990, Asu demanded that the Assam Accord be implemented
 iske baad 17 november, 1999 ko hue tripaksheeya samjhaute main enarasi ko apadet karne kaa nirnay liya
 During the Manmohan Singh era, the government of Manjuritiya approved an amount of Rs 20 crore for the initial work
 lekin kai vajahon se yah kaam shuru nahin ho paaya
 Subsequently, it was approved to update the NRC in the tripartite agreement signed on 5 May 2005 under Manmohan Singh's tenure
 lekin kaam kuch khaas aage nahin badha
 Then after a tripartite meeting on 22 April 2010, the pilot project started in Chaygaon and Barpeta Circle in the state
 upie sarkaar ne di pratik hajela ko jimmedaariakhirkaar maujuuda prakriyaupie sarkaarake samay hi saal 2013 main shuru hui, jab pratik hajela ko enarasi apadet karke liye state koordinator banaaya gaya
 But the actual work gained momentum in February 2015 when the process of setting up NRC service centers started and 6
 6 karod dastavejon ke saath enarasi main naam daalane ke liye 3
 29 crore people applied
 supreme court kaa nirdevgast 2014 main supreme court ne assam sarkaar ko enarasi apadation kii puri prakriya ko teen saal ke bheetar puraa karne kaa aadesh diya tha
 The central government sanctioned Rs 288 crore to update this register
 biharmen suraksha balon ne shuukravaar ko naksaliyon ke thikaane se nau pressure cooker bam evam chah improvizd explosive divaais (iidi) baraamad kiye

 siarpief ke mahanideshak em

 unhone kaha, 'siarpief naksaliyon ke khilaaf talaashi abhiyaan jari rakhegi
 We will take out the Naxalites hiding in the forests and hilly areas
 sinha ne kaha ki chah sainikon kii maut se naksaliyon ke khilaaf siarpief kaa abhiyaan prabhavit nahin hoga
 Here, Additional Director General of Police (law and Order) S
 ke
 Bhardwaj said that the operation against Naxalite organizations will continue
 isamen bihar police, cobra or vishesh kaary bal ke atirikt siarpief ko lagaaya gaya he
 It is noteworthy that Maoists blew up a CRPFK vehicle from a landmine near barha-chakarbanda in Gaya district on Thursday, in which six soldiers were killed and eight policemen were injured
 haryana main trishanku miltaa dikh rahaa janadeshcangress kii doguni ho sakati hai vidhansabhasitaharyana vidhansabha chunaav ke nattejey aa gaye he

 haalanki bijepi 40 siton ke saath sabase badi party ke taur par ubhari he

 The Congress high command has decided to make Bhupendra Singh Hooda the face in Haryana and Kumari Selja as state president just 15 days before the assembly election announcement
 aise main sawaal uthta he ki sonia gandhi party or putr rahul gandhi ke moh main fansi rahi, jiske chalate bhupendra singh hooda par bharosa jataane main kaaphi der kar di
 Explain that in the 2014 assembly elections, BJP got 47 seats, Congress 15, INLD 19 and others 9 seats
 dilachasp baat ye he ki 2014 ke vidhansabha chunaav ke baad se bhupendra singh hooda haryana tatkaaleen pradesh adhyaksh rahe ashok tanvar ko hataane kii maang karte rahe, lekin rahul gandhi ke kareebi hone ke chalate congress sheersh netritv ise najar andaaj karata rahaa

 On 4 September, Congress President Sonia Gandhi decided to enter the electoral arena with the face of Bhupendra Hooda's face in Haryana
 haryana main hooda ko congress pratyaashiyon ke chayan se lekar chunaav main har faisle ke liye puri chhot di gai

 During Sonia Gandhi's tenure, the oldest party in the country remained in power for 10 years, but nothing good was happening for the party in the last 3 years and not only its condition at the center deteriorated but its power from the states one by one
 Kept going aaj sthiti yah he ki congress mahaj 4 rajyon main satta main he
 Rahul commanded the Congress during the Gujarat elections and campaigned in an aggressive manner, presenting himself as a strong leader
 gujarat chunaav se pehle unhen raajnneeti main nausikhia samajha jaataa tha or vipakshi unka jamkar majaak udaate the
 But now the time has changed, he has become the president of the Congress and the party has high hopes from him
 rahul kaa adhyaksh pad par asin hona congress ke liye abhi tak behad shandaar dikh rahaa he
